It is a feelings sensor.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Cats have on an average 24 mystacial whiskers .  These are super antennas\u2014 able to detect depressions in the SPACE TIME FABRIC.   It is alert to slightest stimuli and protects them even while sleeping, as it can sense AURAS ( energy ) and temperature signatures. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The whiskers supplement the cats sense of hearing and sight,  by a strange parallel processing in its brain.  This is the reason why they say the cat has superior hearing sense. Whiskers can sense the air draft caused by sound.  To make your cat blink just touch its whiskers, as they are rooted in a nerve ending and blood vessel rich area. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The cat does NOT like the natural alignment of its whiskers , in place due to electrostatic charge to be disturbed. To feel the ticklish charge just lightly brush your lips or nose tip on the whiskers of your cat. This is the reason if you feed your cat from a narrow mouthed bowl, it will take the food else where.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The whisker hair strand acts as a DIPOLE antenna ( quarter wave rod, representing one half of a dipole , the other ground half being the cat's face ) where HF waves induce weak electrical currents. Cats love to sleep at telluric line crossings.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"querybold\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Cat</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">s are known to have traveled hundreds of miles to find their owners in new homes to which they themselves have never been. -called psi (psychic) trailing.  Scientists have not been able to find a physiological or psychological explanation for this ability. The secret lies in the whiskers. </span></span></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In extremely dim light, a cat may feel its way by using its whiskers.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0in;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The cat uses its whiskers in conjunction with its tail to land on its feet after a jump\u2014 a natural righting reflex.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Mother cats remove the whiskers of the kittens till they are capable of fending for themselves and explore.. He said it spoilt all the expensive matresses and carpets in his house by defecating and urinating on it. And he had to spend nearly one months salary to replace everything. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">I asked him \" Did you make your cat nervous?\"</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">He said \" NO, not at all. But my son had bought a new puppy , as a pet \"</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">I told him  \" This is the way the cat's DNA blueprint is programmed by god. If you make a cat insecure, it will deposit urine and feces around the house to mark its territory. Even rearranging furniture in your house , or a sudden change in routine , will make your cat stressed, leave alone bringing a new pup-- as a cat is a creature of habit!\".</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">After he heard all this, he felt bad.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When a cat falls sick, it will withdraw and be almost lifeless to conserve energy, but will recover sooner than later.. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"></span></span><br />\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Owning a cat is a good forerunner of marriage.
